# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="50168-105">Zastaralé členy v .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="50168-105">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="50168-106">V tomto článku jsou uvedeny členy typu, které jsou zastaralé v .NET Framework 4,5 a novějších verzích.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="50168-106">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="50168-107">Členy typu jsou seskupeny podle sestavení.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="50168-107">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="50168-108">V tomto článku nejsou uvedeny členy zastaralých typů.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="50168-108">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="50168-109">Seznam zastaralých typů naleznete v tématu [zastaralé typy](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="50168-109">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
